/*
root element for scrollable items. Must be absolutely positioned
and it should have a extremely large width to accomodate scrollable
items.  it's enough that you set the width and height for the root
element and not for this element.
*/

/* this cannot be too large */
width:20000em;
position:absolute;
clear:both;
}

root element for the scrollable.

/* required settings */
position:relative;

/* custom decorations */
//border:1px solid #ccc;
//background:url(/media/img/gradient/h300.png) repeat-x;
}
/*
root element for scrollable items. Must be absolutely positioned
and it should have a extremely large width to accomodate scrollable
items.  it's enough that you set the width and height for the root
element and not for this element.
*/
.scrollable .items {
/* this cannot be too large */
width:20000em;
position:absolute;
clear:both;
}
.items div {
float:left;
width:700px;
}

root element for scrollable items. Must be absolutely positioned
and it should have a extremely large width to accomodate scrollable
items.  it's enough that you set the width and height for the root
element and not for this element.

root element for scrollable items. Must be absolutely positioned
and it should have a extremely large width to accomodate scrollable
items.  it's enough that you set the width and height for the root
element and not for this element.

position:absolute;
clear:both;

root element for scrollable items. Must be absolutely positioned

items.  it's enough that you set the width and height for the root
element and not for this element.

/*
root element for the scrollable.
when scrolling occurs this element stays still.
*/
.scrollable {
/* required settings */
position:relative;
overflow:hidden;
width: 700px;
height:320px;
/* custom decorations */
//border:1px solid #ccc;
//background:url(/media/img/gradient/h300.png) repeat-x;
}
/*
root element for scrollable items. Must be absolutely positioned
and it should have a extremely large width to accomodate scrollable
items.  it's enough that you set the width and height for the root
element and not for this element.
*/
.scrollable .items {
/* this cannot be too large */
width:20000em;
position:absolute;
clear:both;
}
.items div {
float:left;
width:700px;
}

//height:495px;
-moz-border-radius:4px;
-webkit-border-radius:4px;
}

border:2px solid #000;
position:relative;
cursor:default;
}

float:left;

element and not for this element.

/*scrollable*/
/*
root element for the scrollable.
when scrolling occurs this element stays still.
*/
.scrollable {
/* required settings */
position:relative;
overflow:hidden;
width: 700px;
height:320px;
/*
root element for scrollable items. Must be absolutely positioned
and it should have a extremely large width to accomodate scrollable
items.  it's enough that you set the width and height for the root
element and not for this element.
*/
.scrollable .items {
/* this cannot be too large */
width:20000em;
position:absolute;
clear:both;
}
.items div {
float:left;
width:700px;
}
/* single scrollable item */
.scrollable img {
float:left;
margin:20px 5px 20px 15px;
background-color:#fff;
width:700px;
//height:495px;
-moz-border-radius:4px;
-webkit-border-radius:4px;
}
/* active item */
.scrollable .active {
border:2px solid #000;
position:relative;
cursor:default;
}
/* this makes it possible to add next button beside scrollable */
.scrollable {
float:left;
}
.browse {
background: url("http://market.poppytalkhandmade.com/ads/blogimages/scrollable/navbar_grey_arrow.png") no-repeat scroll 0 0 transparent;
height: 320px;
left: -1px;
position: absolute;
//top: -1px;
width: 28px;
}
.browse.right {
background-position: -28px 0;
left: auto;
right: -1px;
}

a.disabled {
visibility:hidden !important;
}

color: black;
text-decoration: none;

/*scrollable*/
/*
root element for the scrollable.
when scrolling occurs this element stays still.
*/
.scrollable {
/* required settings */
position:relative;
overflow:hidden;
width: 700px;
height:320px;
/*
root element for scrollable items. Must be absolutely positioned
and it should have a extremely large width to accomodate scrollable
items.  it's enough that you set the width and height for the root
element and not for this element.
*/
.scrollable .items {
/* this cannot be too large */
width:20000em;
position:absolute;
clear:both;
}
.items div {
float:left;
width:700px;
}
/* single scrollable item */
.scrollable img {
float:left;
margin:20px 5px 20px 15px;
background-color:#fff;
width:700px;
//height:495px;
-moz-border-radius:4px;
-webkit-border-radius:4px;
}
/* active item */
.scrollable .active {
border:2px solid #000;
position:relative;
cursor:default;
}
/* this makes it possible to add next button beside scrollable */
.scrollable {
float:left;
}
.browse {
background: url("http://market.poppytalkhandmade.com/ads/blogimages/scrollable/navbar_grey_arrow.png") no-repeat scroll 0 0 transparent;
height: 320px;
left: -1px;
position: absolute;
//top: -1px;
width: 28px;
}

}

/*scrollable*/
/*
root element for the scrollable.
when scrolling occurs this element stays still.
*/
.scrollable {
/* required settings */
position:relative;
overflow:hidden;
width: 700px;
height:320px;
/*
root element for scrollable items. Must be absolutely positioned
and it should have a extremely large width to accomodate scrollable
items.  it's enough that you set the width and height for the root
element and not for this element.
*/
.scrollable .items {
/* this cannot be too large */
width:20000em;
position:absolute;
clear:both;
}
.items div {
float:left;
width:700px;
}
/* single scrollable item */
.scrollable img {
float:left;
margin:20px 5px 20px 15px;
background-color:#fff;
width:700px;
//height:495px;
-moz-border-radius:4px;
-webkit-border-radius:4px;
}
/* active item */
.scrollable .active {
border:2px solid #000;
position:relative;
cursor:default;
}
/* this makes it possible to add next button beside scrollable */
.scrollable {
float:left;
}
.browse {
background: url("http://market.poppytalkhandmade.com/ads/blogimages/scrollable/navbar_grey_arrow.png") no-repeat scroll 0 0 transparent;
height: 320px;
left: -1px;
position: absolute;
//top: -1px;
width: 28px;
}

left: auto;
right: -1px;

element and not for this element.

                <div class="date-outer">
                 <h2 class="date-header">
                  <span>
                   15.2.13
                  </span>
                 </h2>
                 <div class="date-posts">
                  <div class="post-outer">
                   <div class="post hentry" itemprop="blogPost" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
                    <meta content="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-rZHKYsgH32A/UR73LhsIxlI/AAAAAAAA4bQ/huxGHn8loJo/s1600/Screen-shot-2013-02-15-at-6.59.30-PM.jpg" itemprop="image_url"/>
                    <meta content="11678202" itemprop="blogId"/>
                    <meta content="2216098174144539312" itemprop="postId"/>
                    <a name="2216098174144539312">
                    </a>
                    <h3 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name">
                     <a class="comment-bubble" href="https://www.blogger.com/comment.g?blogID=11678202&amp;postID=2216098174144539312&amp;isPopup=true" onclick='javascript:window.open(this.href, "bloggerPopup", "toolbar=0,location=0,statusbar=1,menubar=0,scrollbars=yes,width=640,height=500"); return false;' style="color: #000; font-size: 18px; font-weight: bold;">
                      22
                     </a>
                     Weekend Project: A Crazy Pom Pom Rug
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-2216098174144539312" itemprop="description articleBody">
                     <div dir="ltr" style="text-align: left;" trbidi="on">
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-rZHKYsgH32A/UR73LhsIxlI/AAAAAAAA4bQ/huxGHn8loJo/s1600/Screen-shot-2013-02-15-at-6.59.30-PM.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                        <img border="0" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-rZHKYsgH32A/UR73LhsIxlI/AAAAAAAA4bQ/huxGHn8loJo/s1600/Screen-shot-2013-02-15-at-6.59.30-PM.jpg"/>
                       </a>
                      </div>
                      <br/>
                      <a href="http://meetmeatmikes.com/" target="_blank">
                       Pip Lincolne
                      </a>
                      has a fun and crazy (and I bet soft) pom pom rug project in the latest issue of
                      <a href="http://www.frankie.com.au/" target="_blank">
                       Frankie Magazine
                      </a>
                      - that I'm loving! She says it's "easier than skinning a fraggle" (not sure what that is - but we believe her) and is made with obviously a heap of pom poms attached to a piece of hessian (which I think in North American terms is either burlap or sisal). Whatever the case it's a fun piece and one I wouldn't mind wiggling my toes into first thing in the morning. I grabbed my digital issue of Frankie Magazine from Zinio. Click
                      <a href="http://ca.zinio.com/search/index.jsp?pageRequested=1&amp;showTitles=limit&amp;newsstandSearch=true&amp;predict=true&amp;flag=home&amp;s=frankie&amp;button.x=0&amp;button.y=0" target="_blank">
                       here
                      </a>
                      to pick up a copy. (Photo | Hilary Walker).
                     </div>
                     <div style="clear: both;">
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-footer">
                     <div class="post-footer-line post-footer-line-1">

                        <abbr class="published" itemprop="datePublished" title="2013-02-15T21:01:00-08:00">
                         9:01 p.m.
                        </abbr>
                       </a>

                      <dd class="comment-body" id="Blog1_cmt-6183796286906971466">
                       <p>
                        Fraggles are muppets from Fraggle Rock - it was a TV show ("let the music play, worries for another day, chase your cares away, down at Fraggle Rock" ...  it was on TV when I was younger, I think we have a series on DVD now for my kids).
                        <br/>
                        <br/>
                        And hessian is a really heavy brown, scratchy, hairy, canvassy fabric - it's made into sacks to carry really heavy things ... like lots of potatoes maybe.  I think it's like burlap, like you said.
                        <br/>
                        <br/>
                        I'm in Australia and picked up my copy of Frankie yesterday - Pip's crazy rug is a must-make, it looks so fun and awesome!  Cat
                        <br/>
                        <br/>
